    // language: metal3.1
    #include <metal_stdlib>
    #include <simd/simd.h>
    
    using metal::uint;
    struct DefaultConstructible {
        template<typename T>
        operator T() && {
            return T {};
        }
    };
    
    struct VertexOutput {
        metal::float2 tex_coord;
        char _pad1[8];
        metal::float4 color;
        metal::float4 position;
    };
    struct Locals {
        metal::float2 screen_size;
        metal::uint2 _padding;
    };
    
    metal::float3 linear_from_gamma_rgb(
        metal::float3 srgb
    ) {
        metal::bool3 cutoff = srgb < metal::float3(0.04045);
        metal::float3 lower = srgb / metal::float3(12.92);
        metal::float3 higher = metal::pow((srgb + metal::float3(0.055)) / metal::float3(1.055), metal::float3(2.4));
        return metal::select(higher, lower, cutoff);
    }
    
    metal::float3 gamma_from_linear_rgb(
        metal::float3 rgb
    ) {
        metal::bool3 cutoff_1 = rgb < metal::float3(0.0031308);
        metal::float3 lower_1 = rgb * metal::float3(12.92);
        metal::float3 higher_1 = (metal::float3(1.055) * metal::pow(rgb, metal::float3(0.41666666))) - metal::float3(0.055);
        return metal::select(higher_1, lower_1, cutoff_1);
    }
    
    metal::float4 gamma_from_linear_rgba(
        metal::float4 linear_rgba
    ) {
        metal::float3 _e2 = gamma_from_linear_rgb(linear_rgba.xyz);
        return metal::float4(_e2, linear_rgba.w);
    }
    
    metal::float4 unpack_color(
        uint color
    ) {
        return metal::float4(static_cast<float>(color & 255u), static_cast<float>((color >> 8u) & 255u), static_cast<float>((color >> 16u) & 255u), static_cast<float>((color >> 24u) & 255u)) / metal::float4(255.0);
    }
    
    metal::float4 position_from_screen(
        metal::float2 screen_pos,
        constant Locals& r_locals
    ) {
        float _e7 = r_locals.screen_size.x;
        float _e17 = r_locals.screen_size.y;
        return metal::float4(((2.0 * screen_pos.x) / _e7) - 1.0, 1.0 - ((2.0 * screen_pos.y) / _e17), 0.0, 1.0);
    }
    
    struct vs_mainInput {
        metal::float2 a_pos [[attribute(0)]];
        metal::float2 a_tex_coord [[attribute(1)]];
        uint a_color [[attribute(2)]];
    };
    struct vs_mainOutput {
        metal::float2 tex_coord [[user(loc0), center_perspective]];
        metal::float4 color [[user(loc1), center_perspective]];
        metal::float4 position [[position]];
    };
    vertex vs_mainOutput vs_main(
      vs_mainInput varyings [[stage_in]]
    , constant Locals& r_locals [[buffer(0)]]
    ) {
        const auto a_pos = varyings.a_pos;
        const auto a_tex_coord = varyings.a_tex_coord;
        const auto a_color = varyings.a_color;
        VertexOutput out = {};
        out.tex_coord = a_tex_coord;
        metal::float4 _e6 = unpack_color(a_color);
        out.color = _e6;
        metal::float4 _e8 = position_from_screen(a_pos, r_locals);
        out.position = _e8;
        VertexOutput _e9 = out;
        const auto _tmp = _e9;
        return vs_mainOutput { _tmp.tex_coord, _tmp.color, _tmp.position };
    }

    ) {
        float _e7 = r_locals.screen_size.x;
        float _e17 = r_locals.screen_size.y;
        return metal::float4(((2.0 * screen_pos.x) / _e7) - 1.0, 1.0 - ((2.0 * screen_pos.y) / _e17), 0.0, 1.0);
    }
    
    struct fs_main_gamma_framebufferInput {
        metal::float2 tex_coord [[user(loc0), center_perspective]];
        metal::float4 color [[user(loc1), center_perspective]];
    };
    struct fs_main_gamma_framebufferOutput {
        metal::float4 member [[color(0)]];
    };
    fragment fs_main_gamma_framebufferOutput fs_main_gamma_framebuffer(
      fs_main_gamma_framebufferInput varyings [[stage_in]]
    , metal::float4 position [[position]]
    , metal::texture2d<float, metal::access::sample> r_tex_color [[texture(0)]]
    , metal::sampler r_tex_sampler [[sampler(0)]]
    ) {
        const VertexOutput in_1 = { varyings.tex_coord, {}, varyings.color, position };
        metal::float4 tex_linear = r_tex_color.sample(r_tex_sampler, in_1.tex_coord);
        metal::float4 _e5 = gamma_from_linear_rgba(tex_linear);
        metal::float4 out_color_gamma = in_1.color * _e5;
        return fs_main_gamma_framebufferOutput { out_color_gamma };
    }
